info:Stayed in October 2023

posted:Posted October 24, 2023
msg:The twin sharing suite room is very spacious and comfortable. Bedroom and living room is separated, air-con is strong enough which we like it very much cos although the weather outside is cooling but in the room, we still need the aircon, unlike some other hotels will off the air-con. We like the room's lighting on/off point, that is more considerate as compared to other hotel. They have separated each lighting point and not 1 button off all lights. There's a small kitchen with electric stove, microwave and washing machine provided too. If hotel could provide pot and a small bottle of dish wash will be a plus point. The minus point is the pillow is too soft, we have stacked 2 pillows  but still not firm enough and also the floor tiles in the toilet has dropped off in pieces. Initially, we thought it was dust. However, overall is a satisfied stay. Location of the hotel is very convenient, there're 2 convenient stores opposite the hotel, about 2 -3 mins walk, there are restaurants. The iconic world largest Starbucks ~ Starbucks Reserve Roastery in Shanghai is just 5mins walk away from the hotel. There are nearby huge shopping malls and eatery places, food market, bakery shop as cafe as well as the metro train station.

msg:I was a little disappointed in the hotel. The room didn't match the pictures on the website. Arranged in a corridor style it felt much smaller than the advertised size. 
Due to covid regulations in Shanghai at the time, room service and cleaning was not permitted, which I understand was out of the hotel's control. However, the room was not cleaned properly before check-in and was quite dusty. In general, the room also seemed like it had seen better days with many stuffs and marks. 
The reception area gives a good first impression and staff were polite and helpful when needed.
Despite covid restrictions being lifted by the time of my visit, the swimming pool was closed due to covid, but having seen the pool I may not have wished to swim there anyway. The gym was well equipped but old. The benefit of the hotel is it's location a 5-10 minute walk from a major metro interchange and many shops/restaurants. However, I expected more for the price.
